Client/server compatibility for U2F challenge negotiation\nfunc TestRegression(t *testing.T) {\n\tctx := context.Background()\n\tutils.InitLoggerForTests(testing.Verbose())\n\n\t// Setup: Create auth server with U2F enabled\n\tbk, err := memory.New(memory.Config{})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tclusterName, err := services.NewClusterName(services.ClusterNameSpecV2{\n\t\tClusterName: \"test.localhost\",\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tauthConfig := &auth.InitConfig{\n\t\tClusterName:            clusterName,\n\t\tBackend:                bk,\n\t\tAuthority:              testauthority.New(),\n\t\tSkipPeriodicOperations: true,\n\t}\n\tserver, err := auth.NewServer(authConfig)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Enable U2F in auth preferences\n\tauthPref, err := services.NewAuthPreference(services.AuthPreferenceSpecV2{\n\t\tType:         teleport.U2F,\n\t\tSecondFactor: teleport.U2F,\n\t\tU2F: &types.U2F{\n\t\t\tAppID: \"https://localhost\",\n\t\t\tFacets: []string{\n\t\t\t\t\"https://localhost\",\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t},\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\terr = server.SetAuthPreference(ctx, authPref)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Create a user\n\tuser, err := services.NewUser(\"testuser\")\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tuser.SetRoles([]string{\"admin\"})\n\terr = server.UpsertUser(user)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Set password for the user\n\terr = server.UpsertPassword(\"testuser\", []byte(\"password\"))\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tt.Run(\"MultiDeviceU2FChallenges\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\ttestMultiDeviceU2FChallenges(t, ctx, server, \"testuser\")\n\t})\n\n\tt.Run(\"MFADeviceManagement\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\ttestMFADeviceManagement(t, ctx, server, \"testuser\")\n\t})\n\n\tt.Run(\"ClientServerCompatibility\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\ttestClientServerCompatibility(t, ctx, server, \"testuser\")\n\t})\n}\n\n// testMultiDeviceU2FChallenges verifies that when a user has multiple U2F devices,\n// the server correctly generates challenges for all of them.\nfunc testMultiDeviceU2FChallenges(t *testing.T, ctx context.Context, server *auth.Server, username string) {\n\t// Create two U2F device registrations\n\tdevice1, err := createMockU2FDevice(ctx, server, username, \"device1\")\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\trequire.NotNil(t, device1)\n\n\tdevice2, err := createMockU2FDevice(ctx, server, username, \"device2\")\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\trequire.NotNil(t, device2)\n\n\t// Verify both devices are registered\n\tdevices, err := server.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\trequire.Equal(t, 2, len(devices), \"Expected 2 U2F devices to be registered\")\n\n\t// Request U2F sign challenge (authentication)\n\tchallenge, err := server.U2FSignRequest(username, []byte(\"password\"))\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\trequire.NotNil(t, challenge)\n\n\t// BUG: The Challenges array should contain challenges for BOTH devices\n\t// Currently, the code may only return one challenge\n\trequire.Greater(t, len(challenge.Challenges), 0, \"Expected at least one U2F challenge\")\n\n\t// EXPECTED: With multiple devices registered, we should have multiple challenges\n\t// This test will fail if the server only returns a single challenge when multiple\n\t// devices are registered.\n\tif len(challenge.Challenges) < 2 {\n\t\tt.Logf(\"BUG DETECTED: Expected %d challenges (one per device), but got %d\",\n\t\t\t2, len(challenge.Challenges))\n\t\tt.Fail()\n\t}\n\n\t// Verify each challenge has the required fields\n\tfor i, ch := range challenge.Challenges {\n\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.Challenge, \"Challenge %d: Challenge field should not be empty\", i)\n\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.AppID, \"Challenge %d: AppID field should not be empty\", i)\n\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.KeyHandle, \"Challenge %d: KeyHandle field should not be empty\", i)\n\t}\n\n\t// Verify backward compatibility: the embedded AuthenticateChallenge should be set\n\t// (for compatibility with pre-6.0 clients)\n\trequire.NotNil(t, challenge.AuthenticateChallenge,\n\t\t\"Embedded AuthenticateChallenge should be set for backward compatibility\")\n}\n\n// testMFADeviceManagement verifies that adding and removing multiple devices works correctly\nfunc testMFADeviceManagement(t *testing.T, ctx context.Context, server *auth.Server, username string) {\n\t// Start with one device\n\tdevice1, err := createMockU2FDevice(ctx, server, username, \"mgmt-device1\")\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tdevices, err := server.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tinitialCount := len(devices)\n\n\t// Add a second device\n\tdevice2, err := createMockU2FDevice(ctx, server, username, \"mgmt-device2\")\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tdevices, err = server.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\trequire.Equal(t, initialCount+2, len(devices),\n\t\t\"Expected one additional device after registration\")\n\n\t// Add a third device\n\tdevice3, err := createMockU2FDevice(ctx, server, username, \"mgmt-device3\")\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tdevices, err = server.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\trequire.Equal(t, initialCount+3, len(devices),\n\t\t\"Expected two additional devices after second registration\")\n\n\t// Verify all three devices are distinct\n\trequire.NotEqual(t, device1.GetName(), device2.GetName())\n\trequire.NotEqual(t, device2.GetName(), device3.GetName())\n\trequire.NotEqual(t, device1.GetName(), device3.GetName())\n\n\t// Delete the first device\n\terr = server.DeleteMFADevice(ctx, username, device1.GetName())\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tdevices, err = server.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\trequire.Equal(t, initialCount+2, len(devices),\n\t\t\"Expected device count to decrease after deletion\")\n\n\t// Verify the deleted device is gone\n\tfor _, dev := range devices {\n\t\trequire.NotEqual(t, device1.GetName(), dev.GetName(),\n\t\t\t\"Deleted device should not be in the list\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Verify remaining devices are still there\n\tfoundDevice2 := false\n\tfoundDevice3 := false\n\tfor _, dev := range devices {\n\t\tif dev.GetName() == device2.GetName() {\n\t\t\tfoundDevice2 = true\n\t\t}\n\t\tif dev.GetName() == device3.GetName() {\n\t\t\tfoundDevice3 = true\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\trequire.True(t, foundDevice2, \"Device 2 should still be registered\")\n\trequire.True(t, foundDevice3, \"Device 3 should still be registered\")\n}\n\n// testClientServerCompatibility tests backward compatibility when clients and servers\n// have different versions regarding multi-device U2F support\nfunc testClientServerCompatibility(t *testing.T, ctx context.Context, server *auth.Server, username string) {\n\t// Create two devices\n\tdevice1, err := createMockU2FDevice(ctx, server, username, \"compat-device1\")\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tdevice2, err := createMockU2FDevice(ctx, server, username, \"compat-device2\")\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Get the challenge from the server (new format with multiple Client/server compatibility for U2F challenge negotiation\nfunc TestRegression(t *testing.T) {\n\tctx := context.Background()\n\tutils.InitLoggerForTests(testing.Verbose())\n\n\t// Setup: Create auth \"test.localhost\",\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tauthConfig := &InitConfig{\n\t\tClusterName:            clusterName,\n\t\tBackend:                bk,\n\t\tAuthority:              testauthority.New(),\n\t\tSkipPeriodicOperations: true,\n\t}\n\tserver, err := NewServer(authConfig)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Enable U2F in auth preferences\n\tauthPref, err := services.NewAuthPreference(services.AuthPreferenceSpecV2{\n\t\tType:         teleport.U2F,\n\t\tSecondFactor: teleport.U2F,\n\t\tU2F: &types.U2F{\n\t\t\tAppID: \"https://localhost\",\n\t\t\tFacets: []string{\n\t\t\t\t\"https://localhost\",\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t},\n\t})\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\terr = server.SetAuthPreference(ctx, authPref)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Create a user\n\tuser, err := services.NewUser(\"testuser\")\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tuser.SetRoles([]string{\"admin\"})\n\terr = server.UpsertUser(user)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Set password for the user\n\terr = server.UpsertPassword(\"testuser\", []byte(\"password\"))\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tt.Run(\"MultiDeviceU2FChallenges\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\ttestMultiDeviceU2FChallenges(t, ctx, server, \"testuser\")\n\t})\n\n\tt.Run(\"MFADeviceManagement\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\ttestMFADeviceManagement(t, ctx, server, \"testuser\")\n\t})\n\n\tt.Run(\"ClientServerCompatibility\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\ttestClientServerCompatibility(t, ctx, server, \"testuser\")\n\t})\n}\n\n// testMultiDeviceU2FChallenges verifies that when a user has multiple U2F devices,\n// the server correctly generates challenges for all of them.\nfunc testMultiDeviceU2FChallenges(t *testing.T, ctx context.Context, server *auth.Server, username string) {\n\t// Create two U2F device registrations\n\tdevice1, err := createMockU2FDevice(ctx, server, username, \"device1\")\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\trequire.NotNil(t, device1)\n\n\tdevice2, err := createMockU2FDevice(ctx, server, username, \"device2\")\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\trequire.NotNil(t, device2)\n\n\t// Verify both devices are registered\n\tdevices, err := server.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\trequire.Equal(t, 2, len(devices), \"Expected 2 U2F devices to be registered\")\n\n\t// Request U2F sign challenge (authentication)\n\tchallenge, err := server.U2FSignRequest(username, []byte(\"password\"))\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\trequire.NotNil(t, challenge)\n\n\t// BUG: The Challenges array should contain challenges for BOTH devices\n\t// Currently, the code may only return one challenge\n\trequire.Greater(t, len(challenge.Challenges), 0, \"Expected at least one U2F challenge\")\n\n\t// EXPECTED: With multiple devices registered, we should have multiple challenges\n\t// This test will fail if the server only returns a single challenge when multiple\n\t// devices are registered.\n\tif len(challenge.Challenges) < 2 {\n\t\tt.Logf(\"BUG DETECTED: Expected %d challenges (one per device), but got %d\",\n\t\t\t2, len(challenge.Challenges))\n\t\tt.Fail()\n\t}\n\n\t// Verify each challenge has the required fields\n\tfor i, ch := range challenge.Challenges {\n\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.Challenge, \"Challenge %d: Challenge field should not be empty\", i)\n\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.AppID, \"Challenge %d: AppID field should not be empty\", i)\n\t\trequire.NotEmpty(t, ch.KeyHandle, \"Challenge %d: KeyHandle field should not be empty\", i)\n\t}\n\n\t// Verify backward compatibility: the embedded AuthenticateChallenge should be set\n\t// (for compatibility with pre-6.0 clients)\n\trequire.NotNil(t, challenge.AuthenticateChallenge,\n\t\t\"Embedded AuthenticateChallenge should be set for backward compatibility\")\n}\n\n// testMFADeviceManagement verifies that adding and removing multiple devices works correctly\nfunc testMFADeviceManagement(t *testing.T, ctx context.Context, server *auth.Server, username string) {\n\t// Start with one device\n\tdevice1, err := createMockU2FDevice(ctx, server, username, \"mgmt-device1\")\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tdevices, err := server.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tinitialCount := len(devices)\n\n\t// Add a second device\n\tdevice2, err := createMockU2FDevice(ctx, server, username, \"mgmt-device2\")\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tdevices, err = server.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\trequire.Equal(t, initialCount+2, len(devices),\n\t\t\"Expected one additional device after registration\")\n\n\t// Add a third device\n\tdevice3, err := createMockU2FDevice(ctx, server, username, \"mgmt-device3\")\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tdevices, err = server.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\trequire.Equal(t, initialCount+3, len(devices),\n\t\t\"Expected two additional devices after second registration\")\n\n\t// Verify all three devices are distinct\n\trequire.NotEqual(t, device1.GetName(), device2.GetName())\n\trequire.NotEqual(t, device2.GetName(), device3.GetName())\n\trequire.NotEqual(t, device1.GetName(), device3.GetName())\n\n\t// Delete the first device\n\terr = server.DeleteMFADevice(ctx, username, device1.GetName())\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tdevices, err = server.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\trequire.Equal(t, initialCount+2, len(devices),\n\t\t\"Expected device count to decrease after deletion\")\n\n\t// Verify the deleted device is gone\n\tfor _, dev := range devices {\n\t\trequire.NotEqual(t, device1.GetName(), dev.GetName(),\n\t\t\t\"Deleted device should not be in the list\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Verify remaining devices are still there\n\tfoundDevice2 := false\n\tfoundDevice3 := false\n\tfor _, dev := range devices {\n\t\tif dev.GetName() == device2.GetName() {\n\t\t\tfoundDevice2 = true\n\t\t}\n\t\tif dev.GetName() == device3.GetName() {\n\t\t\tfoundDevice3 = true\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\trequire.True(t, foundDevice2, \"Device 2 should still be registered\")\n\trequire.True(t, foundDevice3, \"Device 3 should still be registered\")\n}\n\n// testClientServerCompatibility tests backward compatibility when clients and servers\n// have different versions regarding multi-device U2F support\nfunc testClientServerCompatibility(t *testing.T, ctx context.Context, server *auth.Server, username string) {\n\t// Create two devices\n\tdevice1, err := createMockU2FDevice(ctx, server, username, \"compat-device1\")\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tdevice2, err := createMockU2FDevice(ctx, server, username, \"compat-device2\")\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Get the challenge from the server (new format with multiple devices)\n\tchallenge, err := server.U2FSignRequest(username, []byte(\"password\"))\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Simulate old client behavior: only use the embedded AuthenticateChallenge\n\t// (not the Challenges array). This is what pre-6.0 clients would do.\n\toldClientChallenge := challenge.AuthenticateChallenge\n\trequire.NotNil(t, oldClientChallenge,\n\t\t\"Embedded challenge should be present for old client compatibility\")\n\n\t// Old clients should be able to use the embedded challenge\n\t// and get a response that the server can verify\n\trequire.NotEmpty(t, oldClientChallenge.Challenge)\n\trequire.NotEmpty(t, oldClientChallenge.AppID)\n\trequire.NotEmpty(t, oldClientChallenge.KeyHandle)\n\n\t// Test JSON marshaling/unmarshaling (simulating wire protocol)\n\tchallengeJSON, err := json.Marshal(challenge)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Unmarshal back\n\tvar unmarshaledChallenge U2FAuthenticateChallenge\n\terr = json.Unmarshal(challengeJSON, &unmarshaledChallenge)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\t// Verify the challenges array is preserved\n\trequire.Greater(t, len(unmarshaledChallenge.Challenges), 0,\n\t\t\"Challenges array should be preserved after JSON round-trip\")\n\n\t// The number of challenges should match the number of devices\n\tdevices, err := server.GetMFADevices(ctx, username)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\tu2fDeviceCount := 0\n\tfor _, d := range devices {\n\t\tif d.GetU2F() != nil {\n\t\t\tu2fDeviceCount++\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// BUG: If this fails, it means the server is not returning challenges for all devices\n\tif len(unmarshaledChallenge.Challenges) != u2fDeviceCount {\n\t\tt.Logf(\"BUG DETECTED: Challenge count mismatch. Expected %d challenges (one per U2F device), got %d\",\n\t\t\tu2fDeviceCount, len(unmarshaledChallenge.Challenges))\n\t\tt.Fail()\n\t}\n}\n\n// createMockU2FDevice creates a mock U2F device for testing\nfunc createMockU2FDevice(ctx context.Context, server *auth.Server, username, deviceName string) (*types.MFADevice, error) {\n\t// Create a mock U2F device\n\tmockU2F := mocku2f.NewMockU2F()\n\n\t// Get auth preferences for U2F config\n\tcap, err := server.GetAuthPreference()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, trace.Wrap(err)\n\t}\n\tu2fCfg, err := cap.GetU2F()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, trace.Wrap(err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Create in-memory storage for this registration\n\tstorage, err := u2f.InMemoryRegistrationStorage(server.Identity)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, trace.Wrap(err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Initialize registration\n\tregChallenge, err := u2f.RegisterInit(u2f.RegisterInitParams{\n\t\tStorageKey: username,\n\t\tAppConfig:  *u2fCfg,\n\t\tStorage:    storage,\n\t})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, trace.Wrap(err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Simulate U2F device registration\n\tmockKey, err := mockU2F.RegisterKeyWithChallenge(&tstranexu2f.RegisterRequest{\n\t\tChallenge: regChallenge.Challenge,\n\t\tAppID:     regChallenge.AppID,\n\t})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, trace.Wrap(err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Get the registration response from the mock device\n\tregResp, err := mockKey.RegisterResponse(&tstranexu2f.RegisterRequest{\n\t\tChallenge: regChallenge.Challenge,\n\t\tAppID:     regChallenge.AppID,\n\t})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, trace.Wrap(err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Verify the registration and create the MFA device\n\tdev, err := u2f.RegisterVerify(ctx, u2f.RegisterVerifyParams{\n\t\tDevName:                    deviceName,\n\t\tResp:                       *regResp,\n\t\tChallengeStorageKey:        username,\n\t\tRegistrationStorageKey:     username,\n\t\tStorage:                    storage,\n\t\tClock:                      server.GetClock(),\n\t})\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, trace.Wrap(err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Upsert the device\n\terr = server.UpsertMFADevice(ctx, username, dev)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, trace.Wrap(err)\n\t}\n\n\treturn dev, Client/server compatibility issues for U2F challenge negotiation\nfunc TestRegression(t *testing.T) {\n\tt.Run(\"MultiDeviceU2FChallenges\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\ttestMultiDeviceU2FChallenges(t)\n\t})\n\tt.Run(\"ClientServerCompatibility\", func(t *testing.T) {\n\t\ttestClientServerCompatibility(t)\n\t})\n}\n\n// testMultiDeviceU2FChallenges verifies the bug where multiple U2F devices\n// registered by a user should all receive challenges during authentication.\n//\n// BUG DESCRIPTION:\n// When a user has registered multiple U2F hardware tokens (e.g., two YubiKeys),\n// the server should present authentication challenges for ALL devices.\n// This allows the user to tap whichever device is available.\n//\n// CURRENT BEHAVIOR (BUGGY):\n// The server presents a challenge for only ONE device, requiring the user\n// to have that specific device available, even if they have other registered tokens.\n//\n// EXPECTED BEHAVIOR:\n// The server presents challenges for ALL registered U2F devices in the\n// Challenges array, with the number of challenges matching the number of\n// registered devices.\nfunc testMultiDeviceU2FChallenges(t *testing.T) {\n\t// Simulate having 3 U2F devices registered\n\tdeviceCount := 3\n\tsimulatedDevices := make([]map[string]string, deviceCount)\n\tfor i := 0;
